# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
What's happening here is that electric susceptibility (material response to electric field wave) is dependent on the frequency of the electric field. The way you get the total polarization is then by integrating the Fourier transform of the *frequency domain of the polarization* over all of the frequencies.
 ^5g7zRI56

You are modeling the dipoles as springs, converting to the frequency domain, and then solving for the phasor notation of the polarization as a function of the electric field phasor. ^5mWTay9C

The stiffness constant is needed (express it in frequency) ^cQR2IaR6

%%
